## SASL Mechanism Configuration Validation at Broker Startup

The validation is spread across these Java source files in `apache/kafka`:

### Core Validation Files

1. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/internals/BrokerSecurityConfigs.java`** — Defines `SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG` (`sasl.enabled.mechanisms`) and its default (GSSAPI).

2. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/ChannelBuilders.java`** — Entry point at broker startup (`serverChannelBuilder()`). Reads `sasl.enabled.mechanisms` and calls `JaasContext.loadServerContext()` for each mechanism.

3. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/JaasContext.java`** — **JAAS config presence check**: `loadServerContext()` and `defaultContext()` throw `IllegalArgumentException` if no JAAS config entry is found for a mechanism.

4. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/JaasConfig.java`** — Parses and validates the dynamic `sasl.jaas.config` property.

5. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/SaslChannelBuilder.java`** — **Mechanism-specific validation**: `configure()` and `createServerCallbackHandlers()` dispatch to SCRAM, OAUTHBEARER, GSSAPI, and PLAIN handlers.

6. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerAuthenticator.java`** — **`sasl.enabled.mechanisms` validation**: constructor throws if the list is null/empty.

7. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/LoginManager.java`** — Acquires login managers per mechanism, triggering login validation.

8. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/kerberos/KerberosLogin.java`** — **GSSAPI validati

This is the config definition that drives all downstream validation.\\n\\n2. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/ChannelBuilders.java`**: The `serverChannelBuilder()` method is the main entry point called at broker startup (via `SocketServer`). Its inner `create()` method reads `SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG` and for each enabled mechanism calls `JaasContext.loadServerContext()` to validate JAAS config presence. This is the primary sasl.enabled.mechanisms validation point.\\n\\n3. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/JaasContext.java`**: Contains `loadServerContext()` which performs the JAAS config presence check. For OAUTHBEARER, it defaults to `OAuthBearerUnsecuredLoginCallbackHandler`.\\n\\n8. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/kerberos/KerberosLogin.java`**: GSSAPI-specific validation. The `configure()` method calls `getServiceName()` which validates that a Kerberos service name is defined in either the JAAS config or the Kafka config (`sasl.kerberos.service.name`). Throws `IllegalArgumentException('No serviceName defined in either JAAS or Kafka config')` if missing.\\n\\n9. **`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/OAuthBearerValidatorCallbackHandler.java`**: OAUTHBEARER broker-side validation.
